 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Saurapani village of Gorkha district was also completely destroyed in the horrific earthquake in Nepal on Saturday
 usee gaanv kii rahane vaali sun kumari gurung kaa bhi ghar bukamp kii vajah se dhwast ho chukaa tha
 Sunkumari, lying 9 months pregnant, lay unconscious in the broken debris of her own home
 shaam ko chah baje sthaneey graminon ne sun kumari ko malbe se baahar nikaala or lagaataar aa rahe bukamp kii vajah se paas ke hi torong jangal main le gaye, jahaan sun kumari ne torong jangal kii ek gupha main ek beti ko janm diya, lekin us samay naa to uske paas koi davaaiyaan thi na hi nurse
 Sun Kumari told that at the time of childbirth, neither she had any food to eat, nor hot water medicine to bake is very far away
 sirf pani pikar sunkumari ne chaar din bataae
 On Wednesday, when the helicopter reached her village, the woman was admitted to Gorkha District Hospital
 sun kumari to thik he, lekin uski navjaat beti ko jaundice ho gaya he or uskaa ilaaj chal rahaa he
 There the doctors have said that the girl could not get treatment
 sunkumari ne kaha ki uske paas na to paisa he or na hi koi saadhan, jisase vah duusare aspataal main jaakar ilaaj kara sake
 Sunkumari herself is badly injured due to being buried under debris
 vah khud bhi chal phir nahin sakati or usapar se apni navjaat bacchee ilaaj ke abhaav main or biimaar hoti ja rahi he
 Sunakumari named her daughter Bhuinchampa
 nepali main bhucamp ko bhuinchaalo kehete he
 Since she gave birth to a daughter on the day of the earthquake, she calls her daughter as Bhuinchampa
 sarkari naukariyon ke avasar kam hone or nijee kshetra kaa dayera badhane kii baat ko sweekaar karte hue centre sarkaar ne shanivaar ko kaha ki vah nijee kshetra main naukariyon main aarakshan ke liye lagaataar baatcheet kar rahi he
 Social Justice and Empowerment Minister Kumari Selja said this while replying to the discussion on 'constitution (scheduled Castes) Order (amendment) Bill 2012' in Lok Sabha
 sadan ne is vidheyak ko dhvanimat se paarit kar diya
 He agreed with the concern of the members participating in the discussion on the Bill that non-provision of reservation for Scheduled Castes in jobs in the private sector can cause serious problems
 sailaja ne bataaya ki nijee sector ko is sambandh main kai baar chitthiyaan likhi gai hai or sarkaar chaahati he ki nijee kshetra kisi na kisi tarah se khud is baat ko mahasoos kare ki yah kitna gambhir mudda he
 He said that if the private sector did not take this issue seriously then it could have many consequences
 basapa ke darasingh chouhan dwaara is sambandh main kade kadam uthaae jane kii maang kiye jane par sailaja ne kaha ki sarkaar chaahati he ki kade kadam nahin uthaane paden or acha hoga ki nijee kshetra aaraam se is baat ko maan jaae
 Earlier, starting the discussion, bjp's Virendra Kashyap said that a policy should be formulated to address the issue of who belongs to the Scheduled Castes and who does not
 unhone nyaaypalika main bhi is jati ke logon ke liye aarakshan kaa praavdhaan kiye jane kii apil kii
 PL Poonia of the Congress said that there are more job opportunities in the private sector and that is why the Scheduled Castes should get reservation in this area
 is vidheyak ko saamaajik nyaay mantri kumari sailaja ne 5 agast ko pesh kiya tha
 sp's Shailendra Kumar said that due to lack of facilities to SC or ST, they demand to go from SC to ST or ST to SC
 basapa ke baliram ne nijee kshetra main aarakshan ke liye samvidhan main sanshodhan kii jarurat bataai
 Bhudev Chaudhary of the Janata Dal UK said that 80 percent of SC and ST children are still malnourished due to which they suffer from disability and disease
 tippaniyan Saugata Roy of Trinamool Congress and Mohan Malik of CPI (M) also expressed the need for reservation in the private sector
 bijd ke mohan jena ne kaha ki paramparaagat udyog lupt ho rahe hai or iske chalate anu jati or janajati ke logon ko adhik pareshaaniyon kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 Prabodh Panda of CPI, SD Sharik of National Conference, Asaduddin Owaisi of All India Majlis a Ittehadul Muslimeen, Ajay Kumar of Jharkhand Vikas Morcha (prajatantrik), Raghuvansh Prasad Singh of RJD, Sanjay Singh Chauhan of RLD, Virendra Kumar of BJP and Congress R
 Dhruvanarayan also participated in the discussion
 saamaajik nyaay or aadhikarita mantri kumari sailaja ne loksabhaa main ‘samvidhan (anusuchit jatiyaan) aadesh (sanshodhan) vidheyak 2012’ par hui charchaa kaa jawaab dete hue yah baat kahi
 The House passed this bill by voice
 unhone vidheyak par charchaa main bhaag lene vaale sadasyon kii is chintaa se sahmati jataai ki nijee kshetra main naukariyon main anusuchit jatiyon ke liye aarakshan kaa praavdhaan nahin hone se gambhir samasyaayein paidaa ho sakati hai
 Salja said that letters have been written to the private sector several times in this regard and the government wants the private sector to somehow realize how serious this issue is
 unhone kaha ki nijee kshetra ne is mudde ko gambhirtha se nahin liya to iske kaaphi dushprinaam ho sakate hai
 When demanded by the bsp's Dara Singh Chauhan to take tough steps in this regard, Salja said that the government wants that strict steps should not be taken and it would be better for the private sector to accept this thing comfortably
 isse pehle charchaa kii shuruyaat karte hue bhaajapa ke virendra kashyap ne kaha ki koun anusuchit jati kaa he or koun nahin, is mudde ke samaadhaan ke liye ek niti banani chahie
 He also appealed for the provision of reservation for people of this caste in the judiciary
 congress ke piel punia ne kaha ki nijee kshetra main naukariyon ke adhik avasar hai or isiilie anusuchit jatiyon ko is kshetra main aarakshan milanaa chahie
 The bill was introduced by Social Justice Minister Kumari Selja on 5 August
 sapa ke shailendra kumaar ne kaha ki essi yaa asti ko suvidhaayen nahin milane ke kaaran hi ve log essi se asti yaa asti se essi main jane kii maang karte hai
 bsp's Baliram stated the need to amend the constitution for reservation in the private sector
 janata dal you ke bhoodev choudhary ne kaha ki essi or asti ke 80 fisadi bachche abhi bhi kuposhan kaa shikaar hai jisaki vajah se ve viklaangata or beemaari se grasit rahete hai
 The comments trinmul congress ke saugat raay or makapa ke mohan malik ne bhi nijee kshetra main aarakshan kii jarurat bataai
 Mohan Jena of BJD said that traditional industries are disappearing and due to this people of Anu caste and tribe are facing more problems

 Diwali (diwali 2018) is the biggest festival of Hindus
 diwali kaa tyohaar 5 dinon tak chalata he
 This includes Dhanteras, Narak Chaturdashi, Deepawali, Govardhan Puja and Bhai Dooj
 vahiin 5 dinon tak chalane vaale in tyoharon main sabase ahm teesraa yani badi diwali kaa din hota he
 This time Diwali will be celebrated on 7 November
 diwali ke dinmaa lakshmiki khaas puja kii jaati he
 It is believed that by making Lakshmi ji happy, money can be filled with grains
 dharmik manyata he ki is din maa lakshmi dharti par bhraman kar rahi hoti hai
 The special worship performed on Diwali is actually done to welcome Mother Lakshmi to the house
 aaie jaane maa lakshmi kii puja karte samay kin baton kaa dhyaan rakhana chahie
 
 
 Ingredients for Puja on Diwali: Mahalakshmi Pujan includes saffron, roli, rice, betel leaf, betel nut, fruit, flowers, milk, kheel, betashe, vermilion, dried fruits, sweets, curd, Ganges water incense, incense sticks, Deepak Rui, Kalawa, coconut and a copper vessel for the urn
 jaane kin baton kaa rakhte hue karen puja
 
 
 1
 puja ke din sabase pehle ek badi or saaf chaowkee par laal yaa pilaa kapadaa bicha kar uske upar lakshmi-ganesh kii murtiyon sthapit rakh den
 Keep in mind that they should be facing east or west
 lakshmi ji ko ganesh ji ke dahini ore virajman karen
 2
 pujan karne vaale sabhi logamurtiyonke saamne kii taraf baithen

 dilli ke east uttam nagar metro stesan par yatriyon ne jamkar hangaamaa kiya

 jawan nashe main dhut tha

 patni ne bich bachaav kiya to uske saath bhi badasluki kii

 haalanki mana ja rahaa he ki desh main lakhon upabhokta abhi tak aisa nahin kar paae hai

 jo upabhokta 31 march tak link nahin kara paae hai, unke paas june tak kaa ek mauqaa he

 lekin agar wo july main bharte hai, to sirf ek maheene kii sabsidi hi milegi

 gas conection ko bank acount se link karne kii prakriya bahut hi saral he
 In this, consumers go to their bank account and present Aadhaar card
 sabsidi kaa form bhar kar jamaa karte hai

 iske pehle yaa iske baad upabhokta ko aadhaar card gas agency ke paas pesh kar use gas conection se link karana hota he
 In this way the Aadhaar card gets linked to the bank account on one side and the gas connection on the other side
 silinder lete samay upabhokta ko to bazaar bhav se puure paise dene padate hai, lekin sabsidi kaa paisa unke acount main waapas aa jaataa he

 isliye jinke paas aadhaar card nahin he, wo apane bank main jaakar gas conection ke number se sidhe acount ko link kar sakate hai

 sidhe bank acount main cash sabsidi se ghapale ghotaale kaa andeshe ko khatm karne kii niyat se laayaa gaya he

 hamane rajmauli se kuch khaas baatcheet kii or aapke liye pesh hai usee ke kuch mukhya ansh:lagbhag 318 dinon tak chali is film kii shooting kii taiyaari kitni khaas thi?badi taiyaari kerani padi kyonki is film main 2 pidiyon kii baat kehani thi isiilie hamane do hisson main is film ko relies karne kii sochi he

 film ban chuki acchhee , buree yaa jaisi bhi thi , wo khatm ho gayi, ab nae kaam kii baari he

 to mujhe lagata he ye kahani logon ko pasand aegi

 main fresh film bananaa chaahunga

 What were your favorite directors in your childhood? i did not even know in my childhood that there are any directors in a film
 kaaphi baad main pataa chalaa kii diarector bhi hota he or maine bhi diarector banane kaa khwab dekha

 isiilie ham dabing ke dauraan 2-3 baar check karte hai

 to ham in sabhi baton kaa khyaal rakhte hai

 unki pichhali filmon se mujhe koi fark nahin padataa he
 i only see him in my characters
 bahubali kii tulana bollywood kii filmon 'krish' ityadi se bhi kii ja rahi he?meri film ek superhiro vaali film nahin he

 darshakon ke liye imotional contant he

 kya aap koi mahila pradhan film karnaa chahenge?main kabhi bhi purush yaa mahila pradhan film soch kar nahin banaata

 lekin bahubali main kai mahila kirdaar hai jo ahm role nibhaati hai

 to aisi feeling aati he

 wo bataate hai kii kya acha he yaa kya nahin he

 ye ek diarector kii aankhon se dikhaaya gaya sach hota he
